{"nick":"joepie91","message":"were provided because executing stuff unnecessarily is sometimes cheaper than forcibly executing everything sequentially... except there are a (growing) number of bugs in how the CPU manages memory when it executes stuff out of order, sometimes not correctly clearing caches or checking memory access boundaries when switching between privileged/unpriviliged context, because due to out-of-order execution it can execute unprivileged code while in","date":"2018-06-24T16:20:17.767Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"privileged mode and vice versa","date":"2018-06-24T16:20:19.264Z","type":"message"}
